[30;1m202 | [0m[35mAgain in *uncompyle6* there are lots of grammar rules, so it is very[0m
[30;1m203 | [0m[35measy to have dead grammar rules that never get used. And[0m
[30;1m204 | [0m[35mgrammar constructs from one version of Python can easily bleed into[0m
[30;1m205 | [0m[35manother version. By looking at grammar coverage over a large set of[0m
